Decoder filters are applied in the order they are configured. Encoder filters are applied in reverse order (prepended rather than appended) so that the last configured filter is the outermost in the encoding chain.\\n\\n## Key Interfaces\\n\\n1. **FilterChainFactory** (envoy/http/filter_factory.h:89): Abstract interface with createFilterChain and createUpgradeFilterChain methods. For static filters, a factory callback (FilterFactoryCb, defined in envoy/http/filter_factory.h:24) is created immediately from the proto config.\\n\\n## Execution Flow at Runtime\\n\\n### Filter Chain Creation\\nWhen a new HTTP stream arrives at ConnectionManagerImpl (source/common/http/conn_manager_impl.h), the newStream method is invoked. This creates an ActiveStream which instantiates a FilterManager (source/common/http/filter_manager.h:638-800). The FilterManager implements the FilterChainManager interface (envoy/http/filter_factory.h:70-81).\\n\\nThe HttpConnectionManager's FilterChainFactory implementation (which is the HttpConnectionManagerConfig) calls createFilterChain, which invokes FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.cc:17-47). This utility method:\\n1. Iterates through the stored FilterFactoriesList\\n2. For each filter factory provider, retrieves the actual FilterFactoryCb\\n3. Calls FilterManager::applyFilterFactoryCb (source/common/http/filter_manager.h:697) which applies each factory callback\\n4. Each callback creates filter instances and adds them to the decoder or encoder filter chains\\n\\n### Filter Execution\\nOnce the filter chain is constructed, filters are executed as data flows through the stream:\\n- `decodeHeaders` (line 748): Processes request headers through decoder filters\\n- `decodeData` (line 758): Processes request body through decoder filters  \\n- `decodeTrailers` (line 767): Processes request trailers through decoder filters\\n\\nThe FilterManager maintains separate lists of decoder_filters and encoder_filters (LinkedList structures). Decoder filters are applied in the order they are configured. Encoder filters are applied in reverse order (prepended rather than appended) so that the last configured filter is the outermost in the encoding chain.\\n\\n## Key Interfaces\\n\\n1. **FilterChainFactory** (envoy/http/filter_factory.h:89): Abstract interface with createFilterChain and createUpgradeFilterChain methods. Implemented by HttpConnectionManagerConfig to instantiate filter chains on demand.\\n\\n2. **FilterChainManager** (envoy/http/filter_factory.h:70): Interface for applying filter factory callbacks. Implemented by FilterManager to handle filter instantiation.\\n\\n3. **FilterManager** (source/common/http/filter_manager.h:638): Manages both decoder and encoder filter chains for a single HTTP stream, coordinating data flow through all configured filters.\\n\\n4. **FilterChainHelper** (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h:68): Template utility that processes filter configurations and creates filter configuration providers during setup.\\n\\n5. **FilterChainUtility** (source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.h:42): Static utility providing createFilterChainForFactories method that instantiates the actual filter chain at stream time.\\n\\nThis architecture allows Envoy to:\\n- Support dynamic filter configuration through config providers\\n- Enable per-filter error handling\\n- Maintain filter execution order consistently across requests\\n- Support both statically configured and dynamically discovered filters (ECDS)\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
